<P style="line-height:14pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-size:12pt" align=center><FONT FACE="Times New

<P style="line-height:14pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-size:12pt" align=center><B><U>ENTERRA CONFIRMS 
DECEMBER 2003 DISTRIBUTION</U></B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt"><BR></P>
<P style="line-height:14pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>Calgary, Alberta 
&#150; December 24, 2003</B> <FONT FACE="Symbol">&#190;</FONT> Enterra Energy 
Trust (Nasdaq: EENC and TSX: ENT.UN) today confirms that the cash distribution 
to be paid on January 15, 2004 in respect of the December 2003 production, for 
unitholders of record on December 31, 2003 will be US$0.10 (C$0.13) per trust 
unit. &nbsp;The ex-distribution date is December 29, 2003.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>

<FILENAME>nceacquisition.htm
<DESCRIPTION>NEWS RELEASE
<TEXT>
<!doctype html public "-//IETF//DTD HTML//EN">
<HTML>
<HEAD>
<TITLE>For Immediate Release</TITLE>
<META NAME="author" CONTENT="Compaq User">
<META NAME="date" CONTENT="12/23/2003">
</HEAD>
<BODY style="line-height:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt; 
color:#000000">
<P style="margin:0pt" align=center><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
width:561.6pt"><img src="nceacquisition001.jpg" alt="[nceacquisition001.jpg]" 
align=middle height=42.4 width=214.333></P>
<P style="line-height:14pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-size:12pt" align=center><FONT FACE="Times New 
Roman" COLOR=#000000><B><U>FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</U></B></FONT></P>
<P style="margin:0pt"><BR></P>
<P style="line-height:14pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-size:12pt" align=center><B><U>ENTERRA PURCHASES 
1,800 BOE/DAY OF PRODUCTION</U></B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=center><BR></P>
<P style="line-height:14pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-size:12pt" align=center><B><U>Transaction to 
close January 29, 2004</U></B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt"
align=justify><B>Calgary, Alberta &#150; December 23, 2003</B> <FONT 
FACE="Symbol">&#190;</FONT> Enterra Energy Trust (Nasdaq: EENC and TSX: ENT.UN) 
today announced it has signed a purchase and sale agreement for the acquisition 
of several properties in East Central Alberta for US$15 million (C$20 million). 
&nbsp;These properties currently produce approximately 1,800 boe/day, consisting
of 1,600 bbls/day of oil and 1,200 mcf/day of natural gas, along with 
approximately 22,166 acres of undeveloped land.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt"
align=justify>&#147;The acquisition of these properties will provide Enterra 
with an opportunity for growth in 2004 through additional optimization and 
development&#148; said Luc Chartrand, President and CEO of Enterra. 
&nbsp;&#147;The addition of these assets to our current inventory of properties 
is expected to be very accretive in terms of cash flow and earnings for 
2004.&#148; </P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt"
align=justify>Funding for this acquisition will be obtained through a 
combination of equity and debt financing.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt"
align=justify>Enterra is currently assessing the opportunities to enhance the 
production for these properties through selective optimization and additional 
drilling in 2004. &nbsp;This development program will begin in February 2004. 
</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt"
align=justify>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt"
align=justify><U>January distribution</U></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt"
align=justify>Enterra Energy Trust will commence its monthly distributions on 
January 15, 2004. &nbsp;The amount will be US$0.10 per trust unit. &nbsp;The ex-
dividend date is December 29, 2003.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt"
align=justify><U>Insider stock sales policy</U></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
width:561.6pt">Enterra has instituted a series of internal guidelines for all of
its executives and directors. &nbsp;The policy will limit insider sales to a 30-
day period following the filing of quarterly and year-end reporting. 
&nbsp;&#147;Enterra does not currently have a formal program in place, so these 
guidelines will set up the parameters for all insider sales going forward.&#148;
added Mr. Chartrand. </P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt"
align=justify><I>Statements regarding anticipated oil and gas production and 
other oil and gas operating activities, including the costs and timing of those 
activities, are &quot;forward-looking statements&quot;. &nbsp;These statements 
involve risks that could significantly impact the Company. &nbsp;These risks 
include, but are not limited to, adverse general economic conditions, operating 
hazards, drilling risks, inherent uncertainties in interpreting engineering and 
geologic data, competition, reduced availability of drilling and other well 
services, fluctuations in oil and gas prices and prices for drilling and other 
well services and government regulation and foreign political risks, as well as 
other risks commonly associated with the exploration and development of oil and 
gas properties.</I></P>
<P style="margin:0pt" align=justify><BR></P>
